1. The hotel environment is not bad even if it is said to be the core of the scenic spot. It is the only hotel with a swimming pool in the scenic spot. The scenic spot is not big, and it takes about 40 minutes to walk around in a circle.
The village is built on two mountains, and the existing village has been artificially transformed. It is not as exaggerated as a summer resort as mentioned in the Little Red Book. It is still hot, but not as hot as the city. After all, the air is still very fresh deep in the mountains. . The room environment is average and the hardware facilities are not complete; except for breakfast, there is no restaurant for lunch and dinner. The only restaurant for dining is the restaurant bar on the swimming pool level. Not to mention the food in it is not suitable for children because it is spicy. The swimming pool is not big, and the water quality can only be said to be okay because there are not many people.
2. The overall service is average, the breakfast is very ordinary and can be full. What makes me more dissatisfied is: 1. Check in at the entrance of Zhaizi Service Center - take the minibus, which must be full before driving, and go to the hotel together. I arrived very late after taking the high-speed train all day, and my kids were fussy. I was really annoyed that after finally arriving to check in, I had to wait for the shuttle bus to be full before I could go to the hotel to get my room card. Check-in is at the entrance of the scenic spot. The hotel is inside the scenic spot and you need to take a shuttle bus, which is very unreasonable. Also, on the first day we checked in, we already asked if we could check out 1-2 hours later because the high-speed train was leaving at 4:30. There was a 3-year-old child who wanted to take a lunch break. We were asked to ask again the next day, and we went the next day. Let's ask again before checking out. I went there on the morning of check-out and was told no, saying that another guest had just been assigned... Why didn't you tell me on the first day.
3. There are not too many businesses in the scenic area, and there are few restaurants. They are all spicy, so it is not suitable for bringing children. The programs in the scenic area are the same every day, and the drones and water shows are not that surprising. Boating is also very cheating. The price is 60/person one way, and you can only go if you have 6 people or more.
